Instead of struggling to remember the correct command and wasting time looking it up on the web, you can turn to a graphical, user friendly and simple interface like Automatic Shutdown.\r\n\r\nAutomatic Shutdown represents a GUI for the Windows automatic shutdown sequence, giving you the possibility to schedule your PC to power off at desired times. \r\n\r\nAnother practical part of this software application is that it gives you the possibility to abort the shutdown operation if you change your mind.\r\nIf you have doubts about the program's functionality (if it's actually working properly), you just have to keep an eye out for Windows built-in notifications, which appear on the lower-right corner on the screen as soon as you set the scheduler or cancel the task (Note it takes a couple of seconds for notifications to update).\r\n\r\nTo sum up, it's a simple and practical autoshutdown utility that's worth keeping in your collection of portable apps for when you quickly have to set a turnoff scheduler and then leave your workstation unattended. It is very powerful and super easy to use. It is fast and capable of loading huge models. It is a great tool for viewing, reviewing and collaborating on 3D assets.\r\n\r\n\r\nMajor Features:\r\n\r\nOpen 3D data file in IGES (.igs or .iges) format\r\n\r\nView models in 3D, spinning, panning, zooming in/out with perspective or orthographic projection\r\n\r\nMeasure distance, location, volume, area, length, radius, angle, boundary and many more\r\n\r\nSupport different rendering mode, support rendering color and background customization\r\n\r\nOpen multiple files in the same window so that you can compare 3D models\r\n\r\nExport in STL, DAE, DXF, OBJ, PLY and ATD formats\r\n\r\nDesigned for Microsoft Modern Style User Interface\r\n\r\nSupport both mouse and touch\r\n\r\nSupport opening 3D files from local drive, email attachments or One Drive\r\n\r\nProvide native zip/unzip support, support loading zipped 3D files directly\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\nThe app is part of ATView3D 3D visualization tool family developed by Afanche Technologies.
